 By following a few simple hair care tips, you can fulfill your dream of getting beautiful hair
 1
 According to skin experts, it is necessary to wash them as soon as they start looking oily
 sir kii twachaa saaf rakhane se roosi bhi nahin hoti tathaa baalo bhi badhate hai
 Hair should be washed twice a week with mild shampoo
 2
 Keep in mind while applying oil, applying oil in hair is very important to nourish them, but this does not mean that you should always keep your hair in oil
 zyada tel lagane se sir kii twachaa ke chhidr band ho jate hai kyonki sir kii twachaa se bhi tel nikalataa he
 Therefore, it is more important to apply more oil to the hair than to apply oil on the scalp
 3
 Avoid using chemical products, sprays and other chemicals used for hair styling spoil hair
 ye baalo kii jhadon ko kamjor bana dete hai jisase bal tuutane jaisi samasyaayein hone lagati hai
 To make a hairstyle, make a pack or mask at home
 4
 Avoid excessive coloring and bleaching of hair
 niyamit taur par inkaa upyog karnaa baalo ko ruukhaa or kamjor bana detaa he jisase baalo patale hone lagate hai
 Use a natural henna to color the hair
 5
 Do not comb wet hair Most women and girls make a mistake in combing wet hair
 aisa karne se bachein
 If the hair is wet, brush them with the help of fingers and comb only when the hair is dry
 6
 Using a hair dryer Sometimes it is okay to use a hair dryer but using it daily brings dryness to the hair
 isliye iskaa upyog kam se kam karne kii koshish karen
